<DIV style="position:absolute;top:193;left:447">(&#8220;AngloGold Ashanti&#8221;
or the &#8220;Company&#8221;)</DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:193;left:696"><font style="line-height:15px;">
<br> </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:230;left:85 "><font style="color:#211e1f;"><b>
</b></font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:250;left:83"><font style="line-
height:20px;"><b> <br>15 August 2016 </b></font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:288;left:83"><font style="font-
size:17.8pt;color:#f5921f;line-height:27px;"><b> <br>NEWS RELEASE 
</b></font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:339;left:83"><font style="line-
height:16px;"><b> <br>AngloGold Ashanti Trebles Free Cash Flow to $108m, Cuts 
Net Debt 32%  <br> <br><i>(JOHANNESBURG &#8211; PRESS RELEASE)-</i> 
</b>AngloGold Ashanti said it more than trebled free cash <br>flow generation in
the first half of the year to $108m and lowered net debt by almost a third, as 
<br>costs fell and it took advantage of a higher gold price. <br> <br>AngloGold 
Ashanti has delivered on a range of self-help measures over the past two years 
to <br>reduce debt using internally generated funds. In focusing on improving 
the quality of its production, <br>the Company has sold some mines, closed 
others and made significant reductions to all areas of <br>cost as it 
prioritises sustainable improvements to free cash flow and returns. <br> 
</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:538;left:83">&#8220;We will continue to push 
hard to improve </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:538;left:364">operational and cost 
performance, as well as our overall </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:554;left:83">balance sheet flexibility, 
regardless of the gold price environment,</DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:554;left:489">&#8221; </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:554;left:517">Chief Executive Officer </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:570;left:83">Srinivasan Venkatakrishnan said. 
&#8220;Our f</DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:570;left:347">ocus remains to improve margins 
and grow cash flow and </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:586;left:83">returns on a </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:586;left:162">sustainable basis.&#8221;</DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:586;left:277"> </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:602;left:83"><font style="line-height:15px;"> 
<br>Net debt fell by 32% to $2.1bn as at June 30 of this year from $3.1bn at the
end of June last year, <br>significantly lowering interest payments. On 1 August
2016, AngloGold Ashanti also completed the <br>redemption of the remaining 8.5%,
seven-year bonds outstanding, at a total cost of the $503m.This extinguished the
C</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:660;left:204">ompany&#8217;s most expensive 
debt and fulfilled a key strategic objective by </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:683;left:83"><font style="line-
height:15px;">further reducing its future interest payments. <br>  <br>All-in 
sustaining costs (AISC) improved to an average of $911/oz in the six months 
through  <br>30 June, compared with the $924/oz recorded in the first half of 
2015.  Production from continuing <br>operations was 1.745Moz, versus 1.878Moz 
in the comparable period last year given the <br>unforeseen challenges faced at 
the Kibali joint venture and planned reduction in output from the <br>Tropicana,
Geita and Obuasi mines. <br> <br></font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:811;left:83">The Company&#8217;s International
Operation</DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:811;left:345">s produced 1.259Moz at AISC of 
$873/oz, accounting for </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:827;left:83"><font style="line-
height:16px;">almost three in every four ounces mined. The performance benefited
from weaker currencies <br>versus the dollar in Argentina, Australia and Brazil.
There were especially strong cost <br>performances from Sunrise Dam and Cerro 
Vanguardia, which posted significant efficiency gains <br>during the first half 
of 2016. <br> <br>A number of brownfield expansion or mine-life extension 
projects are under way, including at <br>Siguiri in Guinea, Sadiola in Mali, 
Tropicana in Australia and Geita, in Tanzania. Pre-feasibility <br>studies of 
two key projects in Colombia are expected to be completed next year, potentially
adding <br>significant new reserves to the C</font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:953 ;left:299">ompany&#8217;s mineral 
inventory.</DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:957 ;left:460"> </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:973 ;left:83"> </DIV>
</DIV>
</FONT><FONT style="font-family:arial;font-size:10.9pt;color:#231f20;"><DIV 
style="position:relative;width:758;height:1073;page-break-before:always;">
<IMG style="position:absolute;top:-2146;clip:rect(2146,758,3219,0)" 
src="anglogold_release001n.gif" alt="background image">
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:45;left:83"><font style="line-height:16px;"> 
<br> <br> <br> </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:109;left:83">AngloGold Ashanti&#8217;s South 
African operations delivered 4</DIV>
<DIV style="position: absolute; top: 109; left: 463px">86,000oz of production at
AISC of </DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:125;left:83"><font style="line-
height:15px;">$958/oz, a 13% cost reduction from the first six months of last 
year. Mponeng, the largest of the <br>local mines, continued its recovery with a
25% jump in output and a 28% reduction in AISC to <br>$893/oz. Tragically, there
were three work-related fatalities at the South African operations during 
<br>the period under review, overshadowing safety improvements that have been 
made across the <br>balance of the portfolio. The South African operations 
continue to face significant challenges due <br>to safety-related stoppages, 
which have continued throughout the year. <br> <br>Adjusted headline earnings 
were $159m, or 39 cents per share in the first half of 2016, compared <br>with 
$61m, or 15 cents per share, in the first half of 2015. Net profit attributable 
to equity <br>shareholders during the first half of 2016 was $52m compared with 
a net loss from continuing <br>operations of $23m a year earlier. <br> 
<br>Adjusted earnings before interest, tax, depreciation and amortisation 
(adjusted EBITDA) <br>decreased by $12m, or 2% from $793m in the six-month 
period ended 30 June 2015 to $781m in <br>the six months ended 30 June 2016. The
lower production year-on-year was largely offset by cost <br>improvements over 
the same period. The ratio of net debt to adjusted EBITDA at the end of June 
<br>2016 was 1.44 times, compared with the 1.47 times recorded at the end March 
2016, and 1.95 <br>times at the end of June 2015, highlighting the success of 
AngloGold Ashanti&#8217;s continued efforts to  </font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:400;left:83"><font style="line-
height:15px;">deleverage and sustainably improve cash flow.  <br> <br> 
<br><b>Ends <br> <br>JSE Sponsor: Deutsche Securities (SA) Proprietary Limited 
<br> <br>Contacts <br> </b></font></DIV>
<DIV style="position:absolute;top:561;left:83"><font style="font-
size:8.5pt;line-height:13px;"><i><b>Media  <br> <br></b></i>Chris Nthite
